Standard capabilities
Addr. ID
----------------
0040  10 = PCI Express
0080  05 = Message Signaled Interrupts, MSI
0090  0D = PCI Bridge Subsystem ID
00A0  01 = PCI Power management

----------------
0100  0001 = Advanced Error Reporting, AER

0A30  0019 = Secondary PCI Express
0A90  0025 = Data Link Feature
0A9C  0026 = Physical Layer 16.0 GT/S
0EDC  0027 = Lane Margining at the Receiver

Standard capabilities
Addr. ID
----------------
0040  10 = PCI Express
0080  05 = Message Signaled Interrupts, MSI
0090  0D = PCI Bridge Subsystem ID
00A0  01 = PCI Power management

----------------
0100  0001 = Advanced Error Reporting, AER
0220  000D = Access Control Services, ACS
0150  001F = Precision Time Measurement, PTM
0A30  0019 = Secondary PCI Express
0A00  001D = Downstream Port Containment, DPC
